plane-crazy 2019-08-31 07:37:06 The fastest self-propelled man-made object was... A manhole cover. It is also the first man-made object to be sent to space. The US government wanted to test what would happen if a nuke was detonated underground, so they dug a huge hole in the ground and put in a nuke, then a thicc concrete layer, then a gap, then the steel manhole cover. The nuke was detonated, vaporizing the concrete and blasting the cover at 125,000 mph, or 34 mps, which is 6x the escape velocity of Earth.
